<rating>1</rating>< Review>
Stopped in this past Saturday around 1 pm. First thing I notice is a sign in the door that says we welcome all religions, races, etc. you are safe here. Ok good to know, got the warm and fuzzy feelings already. No one greeted us as we walked in but the store was cute and had a good variety of food etc..  I picked up a couple of items and then stood in front of the deli case and waited to have my order taken. After a few minutes I turned around and when I turned back around the girl behind the deli counter had started taken another person's order. This person actually stepped in front of me to give her his order. Ok, fine. I was skipped but maybe it was my fault for turning around. I waited again for a few minutes to have my order taken. A group of about 4-5 walked in and we are all waiting to have our orders taken. Another girl walks behind the deli counter and has a conversation with the worker who has been manning the deli. She turns around and completely skips over me and begins speaking to the group who had walked in after I did. I've now been completely ignored twice at the deli and at this point I drop everything in my hands on the counter and walked out. I wasted 15 minutes of an otherwise beautiful day in this place and was left with such a bad taste in my mouth after having been treated as invisible by the people who work here. Fortunately for me, there were lots of other places in the area where I was given great customer service.< /Review>

< Review>
$$$...

Very nice golf course and private club. The grounds are gorgeous all around and the area is one of the premier properties in SoCal; manicured and meticulously maintained. The main stately building is available to public, exceptional restaurant and bar, also seating with appealing views over the golf course both inside and on the patio. Facilities are available for major events and memorable wedding settings. The staff were all very polite and helpful.

I read the reviews as I often do. Most reviewers give high kudos for many of the items I mentioned and much more. There are a few low ratings but I would recommend reading between the lines on these. I didn't find anything whatsoever that I could complain about (but I did not attend or book an event, they can run into difficulties anywhere for sure).

Palos Verdes is fantastic and this gorgeous Golf Course and it's facilities fully live up to high value, love and respect for this expansive lavish parcel of phenomenal real estate.

By:
cmilton111
Google Guide
5.07.2018</Review>

<Text>My experience with PVGC was extremely disappointing.  As President of the Palos Verdes Junior Women's Club, I tried to work with their management to correct the severe service deficiencies we experienced at our Holiday Luncheon Fundraiser held at PVGC on December 3, 2017. The rooms were not set up as promised, there was no English speaking staff on site to assist with issues during the event set up, there were delays in preparation of the dining room, including their inability to find our specialty linens, the custom drinks were not as ordered, and the food was served with an allergen (onions) specifically identified in advance to the catering staff.  We incurred overtime charges from other vendors due to the mismanagement of the staff who was largely absent during our event and when present overtly rude.  Unbelievably, the response from their catering manager, Donna Myers, who was not onsite during our event, was to stonewall and deny all responsibility.
